// ShowErrorAlert(ErrorMessage) // returns undefined
      ShowErrorAlert: function (ErrorMessage)
      {
        var divAlert = $('<div />').attr('id', this.GetRandomAlphaNumericString());

        $(divAlert).addClass('alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom alert-danger ng-scope')
          .css({ 'z-index': 1550, 'cursor': 'pointer' })
          .attr('role', 'alert')
          .append($('<button />')
            .attr('type', 'button')
            .addClass('close')
            .append($('<span />')
              .attr('aria-hidden', 'false')
              .text('x'))
            .append($('<span />')
              .addClass('sr-only')
              .text('Close')))
          .append($('<div />')
            .append($('<div />')
              // .append($('<span />').addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert'))
              // .css({ 'position': 'relative', 'top': '2px' })
              .addClass('ng-scope alert-message')
              .text(ErrorMessage)
              .prepend($('<span />')
                .css('padding-right', '10px')
                .addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert custom-error-icon'))));

        $('body').append($(divAlert).show());
        /*
          <button type="button" class="close" onclick="$(this).closest('div').hide();">
            <span aria-hidden="false">×</span>
            <span class="sr-only">Close</span>
          </button>
          <div>
            <div class="ng-scope alert-message"></div>
          </div>
        */
      }

// Source: Alight Solutions (ALISOL)_DirectToMobileCBR_2434.cs
// function EnableD2MShipping() // returns undefined
function EnableD2MShipping()
	{		
		var userMethodParams = { "ActionMessage": "EnableD2MShipping"};
            
		var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
		
		var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
		
		if (response!=undefined && response.responseJSON.ErrorCode !== 0) 
		{
			alert("Error while executing UserMethod: " + response.responseJSON.ErrorCode);
		}
		else 
		{			
			vm.profile = DecodeReturnString(response.responseJSON.Data);
		}
	}

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns boolean or undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) 
	{
		debugger;
		
		shipmentRequest = SetShipmentRequestUserData(shipmentRequest);
		
		if (CurrentShipmentIsD2M())
		{
			
			var loadedEmailValue = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
			
			if(loadedEmailValue === '')
			{
				alert("Recipient email address is required for Direct to Mobile shipments");
				return false;
			}
			
			SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(true,shipmentRequest);
			
			SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);			
					
			if (shipmentRequest.Packages !== undefined) 
			{
				for (var x = 0; x < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; x++) 
				{
					shipmentRequest.Packages[x].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
					shipmentRequest.Packages[x].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 0;
				}
			}											
		}		
    };

// validateClientMatter() // returns void
function() {

        if( theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference === null) {
            alert('Client Matter field is required. Please enter a valid client matter number!');
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');            
            return;
        }
        
        var cmFound = false;
        var cm = theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        var cmValidationList = theVM.fieldOptions.ShipperReference.FieldOptionValidations;
        for(var i = 0; i < cmValidationList.length; i++) {
            var cmValidationItem = cmValidationList[i];
            if( cmValidationItem.Value == cm) {
                cmFound = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if( cmFound )
            theVM.saveLicensePlate();
        else {
            alert("Client Matter field is invalid. Please enter a valid client matter number!");
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');                        
        }
    }

// handleItemSkuTextChanged(event) // returns void
this.handleItemSkuTextChanged = function(event) {

        var newitemsku = this.Packages[0].MiscReference10;
		if( newitemsku.trim().length === 0 )
			return;

        //debugger;
        
		//alert("Item number: " + orderItemList[1].itemcode + "  qtyordered: " + orderItemList[1].qtyordered + " qtyshipped: " + orderItemList[1].qtyshipped);

		// Check for item code SHIPCOMPLETE indicating that this order is complete
		if( newitemsku == "SHIPCOMPLETE") {

            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Check for SHIP indicating that this box is complete but not the whole order
		if( newitemsku == "SHIP") {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "";		    
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";			
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Pad the input sku to 14 digits with leading zeros
		var skulen = newitemsku.length;
		var newitemskupad = "";
		if( skulen == 6)
			newitemskupad = '00000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 7)
			newitemskupad = '0000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 8)
			newitemskupad = '000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 9)
			newitemskupad = '00000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 10)
			newitemskupad = '0000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 11)
			newitemskupad = '000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 12)
			newitemskupad = '00' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 13)
			newitemskupad = '0' + newitemsku;
		else
			newitemskupad = newitemsku;
			
		newitemsku = newitemskupad;

		//alert("newitemsku: " + newitemsku);

        //alert("orderItemList length: " + orderItemList.length);
        
        //alert("orderItemList itemsku: " + orderItemList[0].itemsku);
       
       //debugger;
       
		// Verify item sku is on this order
		var itemFound = false;
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
		    if( itemFound === true)
		        break;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					itemFound = true;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		
		//alert("itemFound: " + itemFound);
		
		if( itemFound === false) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Error","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
            $("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
            return;			
		}

		// Search for itemcode
		itemFound = false;
		var fullyPacked = false;
		var svSkuCode = "";
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
			if( itemFound == true)
				break;
			
			var nextitem = false;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					if( orderItemList[i].qtyshipped == orderItemList[i].qtyordered ) {
						fullyPacked = true;
						nextitem = true;
						break;
					} else {
						itemFound = true;
						fullyPacked = false;
						var tmpqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyshipped);
						var tmptotqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].totqtyshipped);
						var tmpqtyordered = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyordered);
						if( (tmpqtyshipped + tmptotqtyshipped) < tmpqtyordered) {
							var calcqty1 = tmpqtyshipped + 1 + tmptotqtyshipped;
							var calcqty2 = tmpqtyordered - tmpqtyshipped - tmptotqtyshipped;
							/*alert("Calc quantity 1: " + calcqty1 + " qtyordered: " + tmpqtyordered);*/
							/*alert("Calc quantity 2: " + calcqty2);*/
							if( calcqty1 <= tmpqtyordered) {
								var tmpnewqty = tmpqtyshipped + 1;
								orderItemList[i].qtyshipped = tmpnewqty;
								orderItemList[i].modified = true;
								svSkuCode = newitemsku;
								/*alert("Item added to box ok");*/
							} else {
							    ShowAlert("Pack Error","Scanned quantity for SKU (" + newitemsku + ") would exceed order quantity. Please remove extras from the shipment and try again.");
								$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
                                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                                angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
								return;						
							}
						} else {
							ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
							$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
                            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
							return;						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if( nextitem == true)
				continue;
		}

		if( fullyPacked == true) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
			$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
			vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
			return;					
		}

		$("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	

		//if( itemFound == false) {
		//	ShowAlert("Pack Error 2","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
		//} else {
        //    $("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	
		//}

        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
		}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        var freightfound = 0;
        var frieghterr = 0;

        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) >= 70) {
                freightfound = "1";
            }
            if (freightfound == "1") {
                if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) < 70) {
                    frieghterr = "1";
                }
            }
        }
        if (freightfound == "0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR"
            }
        } else {
            if (frieghterr == "0") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                    Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT"
                }
            } else {
                alert("Cannot create one shipment with 2 different service levels.");
            }
        }
        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol == "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT") {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Packaging = "CUSTOMER_PALLET";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ImportDelivery = true;

        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country == "US") {
            if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == '?') {
                alert("Please confirm shipment value");
                throw ("Excpetion");
            } else {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == "") {
                    if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == 'string:Yes') {
                        alert("Please Enter ITN/ EES number in ConsigneeReference");
                        throw ("Excpetion");
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country != "undefined") {
                alert("For EU Exports : Shipments above 1000 EUR, a formal export declaration is required. A formal electronic export declaration must be sent to customs authorities by the exporter or their representative. Customs authorities grant the release for export and issue an Export Accompanying Document (EAD) with a unique Movement Reference Number (MRN). The EAD has to accompany the shipment. UPS is responsible for the exit clearance at the EU border.")
            }
        }
    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        let confirmReprocess = confirm("Do you want to create more shipments?" + "\n" + " OK = YES and CANCEL = NO");

        if (confirmReprocess) {
            document.location = '#!/shipping';
        } else {
            document.location = '#!/closemanifest';
        }
    }

// Source: Avery Dennison (Avery)_Avery Reference Rule_28.cs
// CheckValidation(checkValue, checkField) // returns the validated value or throws an error
function CheckValidation(checkValue, checkField){
        
        for(var item in checkField){
            if(checkField[item].Value == checkValue)return checkValue;
        }
        throw new Error(checkValue + " is not a valid value.");
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1 !== null)	{
	    if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1.length > 0 ) {
	        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1.substring(0,1) == "~") {
                    shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "ShipExec Alert";
                    shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1.substring(1);
                    angular.element('[ng-model="AlertModalNewShipment"]').modal('show');
	            }
	        else {
                    shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "ShipExec Alert";
                    shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1;
                    angular.element('[ng-model="AlertModal"]').modal('show');
	        }
		}
	}
    }

// Source: BHARTIYA HANDICRAFTS (BHARTIYAHCFT)_ISMEA_FTP_1584.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston Coyol Client Business Rules_2474.cs
// function PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
    if (location === '/shipping') {
       // debugger;
       
       // Get the Logon Profiles Custom Data Values Which Determine the Shipping Options Available to them
        if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === "undefined" || this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === null){
           throw ({ message: 'User Is Missing Required Custom Data Values in Management Studio User Manager Setup Under Address Tab.', errorCode: '' }); 
        }
     
        this.GetCustomDataItems();
            console.log(st_AddressType + ' ' + sf_AddressType + ' ' + uPS_Service + ' ' + return_Type + ' ' + user_description + ' ' + dims + ' ' + user_orderNumber + ' ' + cost_Center + ' ' + user_partNumber + ' ' + insured_Value);
        
        this.ShippingLoaded();
        
        var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
        {
            if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]'))) 
            {
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('#sf_Address').focus();
                $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#svc_select").prop("selectedIndex", 5);
            
                
            }
        }, 400);
        
        //Get Address Book Data
        var addressBookData = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            UserId: client.userContext.UserId
        };
        AddressBooks = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_AddressBook', addressBookData, false).responseJSON;
        AddressBooks.AddressBooks.forEach(item => {
            if(item.Name === "COYOL_ShipToAddress"){
                shipToAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
            if(item.Name === "COYOL_ShipFromAddress"){
                shipFromAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
        });
        console.log("shipToAddressBookId: " + shipToAddressBookId);
        console.log("shipFromAddressBookId " + shipFromAddressBookId);    
        
        //Get the Shipper Account Number from Profile
        this.GetShipperAccount(); 
        console.log(thisShipperAccount);

        this.vm.shipToAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipToAddresses();
        //Setup Ship To Address Drop Down Change Event
       $('body').on('change', '#st_Address', function(e) {             // Not seeing a difference between using either of these as far as GUI reacts.
            var userSelectedShipToCompany = $('#st_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected ShipTo Company :" + userSelectedShipToCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedShipToCompany ==  ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedShipToAddress = ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateShipToAddress();
                }
            } 
            
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                    
                    
                }
            }, 300);
        });

        
        this.vm.returnAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipFromAddresses();
        //Setup Ship From Address Drop Down Change Event
        $('body').on('change', '#sf_Address', function(e) {
            //debugger;
            SelectedReturnAddress = null;
            var userSelectedReturnCompany = $('#sf_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected Return Company :" + userSelectedReturnCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedReturnCompany ==  ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedReturnAddress = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateReturnAddress();
                }
            } 
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
         
        });
        
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]', function(e){
             
            if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount > 2500 ){
                alert('ITN/AES Transaction Number Required');
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
                
            }
        });
        
        
       // $('#billWeight').after('<div id="billable_weight"><strong id="billable_weight_text"></strong></div>');
       // $('#volumetricWeight').after('<div id="custom_volumetric"><span id="volumetric_value_text"></span></div>');
       
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]', function(e){
            // debugger;
              totalShipWeight = 0;
              
              vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
              });
              
              totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
              //console.log(totalShipWeight);
             
              document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
            //debugger;
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
       
    }
};

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    debugger;
    //kg = lbs*0.453592 
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// function RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
}

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    // debugger;
    
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
    //kg = lbs*0.453592    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
    });
    
  
    //cm=in/0.39370
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
       }
         
    });
     
   if(Number(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
};

        }

            console.log(st_AddressType + ' ' + sf_AddressType + ' ' + uPS_Service + ' ' + return_Type + ' ' + user_description + ' ' + dims + ' ' + user_orderNumber + ' ' + cost_Center + ' ' + user_partNumber + ' ' + insured_Value);

            console.log("User Selected ShipTo Company :" + userSelectedShipToCompany);

                    SelectedShipToAddress = ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateShipToAddress();
                }
            }

            if(userSelectedShipToCompany == "BOSTON SCIENTIFIC COYOL"){
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "BS_26737";
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = "26737";

               // };

                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
        });

        $('body').on('change', '#sf_Address', function(e) {

                if(userSelectedReturnCompany ==  ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedReturnAddress = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateReturnAddress();
                }
            } 
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {

                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
         
        });
        
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]', function(e){
             
            if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount > 2500 ){
                alert('ITN/AES Transaction Number Required');
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
                
            }
        });
        
        
       // $('#billWeight').after('<div id="billable_weight"><strong id="billable_weight_text"></strong></div>');
       // $('#volumetricWeight').after('<div id="custom_volumetric"><span id="volumetric_value_text"></span></div>');
       
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]', function(e){
            // debugger;
              totalShipWeight = 0;
              
              vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
              });
              
              totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
              //console.log(totalShipWeight);
             
              document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            //console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            //debugger;
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
       
    }
};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
     // debugger;
     
     totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
     
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// this.RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
}

    function cvsContinue() {
        $('body').delegate('div[ng-if="vm.rateResults.length > 0"] tr td a', 'click', serviceUpgrade)
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.ReasonForUpgrade"]', 'click', function () {
            if (this.value != '?') {
                $('button:contains("Ship")').prop('disabled', false);
            }
        })

        var validateAddressOnRate = getObjectValue(vm.profile.ProfileSetting.ValidateAddressOnRate);
        if (validateAddressOnRate == 'true') {
            $('body').delegate('[ng-click="vm.returnData(button.role)"]', 'click', defaultRateService)
        } else {
            defaultRateService();
        }
    }

// serviceUpgrade() // returns undefined
    function serviceUpgrade() {
        var ignoreReasonService = [
            'UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)'
        ]

        var selectedService = $(this).text();
        var ignoreReason = ignoreReasonService.indexOf(selectedService) >= 0;
        if ($('[ng-model="vm.ReasonForUpgrade"]').val() != '?') {
            $('button:contains("Ship")').prop('disabled', false);
        }

        if (!ignoreReason) {
            $('[name="reasonForUpgrade_txt"]').hide();
        } else {
            $('[name="reasonForUpgrade_txt"]').show();
        }
    }

// getObjectValue(varReference) // returns string

        if(varReference) return varReference;
        return "";
    }

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// SWOGShipment() // returns void
    this.SWOGShipment = function () {
        // Custom function that fires when SWOG button is clicked
        // If Shipper is "MCD" "MCT" or "MCC" there is no validation done on SWOGS and then focus on Dimensions when completed
        
        // Get current Shipper from screen       
        var shipper = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper;        

        debugger;
        // Define initial SWOG array and counter
        var swogArray = ["SWOG_START"];
        var counter = 0;

        // If the masterOrderNumber has an initial SWOG value from PreLoad, push that into the swogArray before collecting new ones.  Set the counter to 1.
        if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
            swogArray.push(masterOrderNumber);
            swogArray = unique(swogArray);
            counter = 1;
        }

        do {
            // Prompt for SWOG data entry until END_SWOG is scanned
            var swog = window.prompt("Enter SWOG order number.  Scan END_SWOG Barcode when complete", "");
            debugger;
            // Make sure swog is not empty
            if (swog != '') {
                if (counter > 0 && swogArray.length > 1) {
                    // This check is only done when the Shipper is NOT MCD, MCT or MCC
                    if (shipper != "MCD" && shipper != "MCT" && shipper != "MCC") {
                        // Make sure the entry is valid (not 'END_SWOG' AND length is greater than 9, not the same as the first entry in the array)
                        if (swog != 'END_SWOG' && swog.length > 9 && swog.substring(0, 9) != swogArray[1].substring(0, 9)) {
                            alert("The order that you scanned = " + swog + " is invalid for this SWOG and will be removed.");
                            swog = '';
                        }
                    }
                }
                // If masterOrderNumber is not empty, this function was called from PreShip.  Otherwise it came from clicking SWOG
                if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
                    // function called from PreShip...validate length of swog
                    if ((swog != '' && swog.length > 9) || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }
                else {
                    // function called from clicking button...do not validate length of swog
                    if (swog != ''  || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }                
            }
        } while (swog != 'END_SWOG');        

        // Put '|' between each SWOG number
        var swogOrderNumbers = "";
        swogArray.forEach(function (item, index, array) { swogOrderNumbers = swogOrderNumbers + "|" + item; });
        swogOrderNumbers = removeFirstChar(swogOrderNumbers);

        // Store final swog data in UserData1
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = 123;
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = swogOrderNumbers;
        this.currentShipment.Packages[0].UserData1 = swogOrderNumbers;

        // If Shipper IS MCD, MCT or MCC then put focus on length field in dimensions
        if (shipper == "MCD" || shipper == "MCT" || shipper == "MCC") {
            lengthText = ('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]');
            setFocus(lengthText);
        }
        // Clear out masterOrderNumber
        masterOrderNumber = "";
        debugger;
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

            }
        })()

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        console.log("PreShip In");

        console.log('paperless:', userParams.paperless);

            var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;

        if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym)) {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
        }
        else {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
        }

        console.log("PreShip Out");
    };

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns constructor function containing alert-related shipment validation
function ClientBusinessRules() {
  var index;
  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
   // alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
    var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
     
  };
  
  this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
      var DIUnit = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Units;
      var DIWt = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Amount;
      var DINote = "Incorrect shipping of Dry Ice can result in fines upward of $75,000 for each violation as well as cancellation of shipping privileges for all of Conagra Brands. Please contact DL-SmallParcelDeliveryService@conagra.com with questions or for specific instructions and restrictions";
   //   alert(DIUnit);
   //   alert(DIWt);
   //   alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight));
  for (var index = 0; index < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ++index) {  
    switch(shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Units) {
      case "LB":
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 5.5) {
            alert(DINote);
            throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
          
        }
      break;
      case "KG":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2.49476) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "G":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2494.76) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "OZ":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 88) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      default:

    }}

    };
  
  
   this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    };
    

   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }
}

// AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = GetShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// Source: CountryMax Stores (CNTM)_CountryMax Shipping CBR_1660.cs
// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;		// autoship
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");
/**

			clearInterval(labelInterval);

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        
        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");
        
        var stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        
        if(customData3=="FC"){
            objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            nameaddress.Account = customData1;
        }
        
        
        function PullCustomData(consignee, field){
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));
            
            for(var item in consignee){
                if(consignee[item].Key==field)return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }
    }

// alert() // returns an object with Info(msg), Success(msg), and Danger(msg) methods
        alert: (function () {
            var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
            var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
            uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

            $('body').append(uibalert);
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

            return {
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }
            }
        })()

// ShowErrorAlert(ErrorMessage) // returns undefined
      ShowErrorAlert: function(ErrorMessage)
      {
        var divAlert = $('<div />').attr('id', this.GetRandomAlphaNumericString());

        $(divAlert).addClass('alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom alert-danger ng-scope')
          .css(
            {
              'z-index': 1550,
              cursor: 'pointer'
            })
          .attr('role', 'alert')
          .append($('<button />').attr('type', 'button').addClass('close')
            .append($('<span />')
              .attr('aria-hidden', 'false').text('x'))
            .append($('<span />').addClass('sr-only').text('Close')))
          .append($('<div />')
            .append($('<div />').addClass('ng-scope alert-message').text(ErrorMessage)
              .prepend($('<span />').css('padding-right', '10px').addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert custom-error-icon'))));

        $('body').append($(divAlert).show());
        /*
          <button type="button" class="close" onclick="$(this).closest('div').hide();">
            <span aria-hidden="false">×</span>
            <span class="sr-only">Close</span>
          </button>
          <div>
            <div class="ng-scope alert-message"></div>
          </div>
        */
      },

            {

                    p.MiscReference4 = ""
                }
            }
        }
    };

            setInterval(function() {

        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }


            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }


            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },
            replaceText2: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerText = this.innerText.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },
             replaceLabel2(selector, oldText, newText) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('label') === oldText) {
                        $(this).attr('label', newText);
                    }
                });
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
            client.init(); 
            clearInterval(intervalId);
        }, 1000);

        switch(location) {
            case '/shipping':
                //this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = "Créer un envoi";
                break;
            case '/history':
                $("h4:first").text("Historique");
                
                break;
            // Add more cases as needed
        }
     }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        canadaSelected = false;
        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
            
            var company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toLowerCase();
            if(company.indexOf("mail innov") != -1 || company.startsWith("ups mi") || company.startsWith("ups mail"))
            {
                if (mi_tpb_stores.find(element => element == this.vm.profile.Shippers[0].Symbol) !== null)
                {
                    console.log("Billing MI as TPB");
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
                    var tpb = {};
                    angular.copy(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee, tpb);
                    tpb.Account = "7500YW";
                    tpb.Company = "UPS MAIL INNOVATIONS";
                    tpb.Contact = "REBECA CARBRERA";
                    tpb.Address1 = "13050 MARLAY AVE";
                    tpb.City = "FONTANA";
                    tpb.StateProvince = "CA";
                    tpb.PostalCode = "92337";
                    tpb.Country = "US";
                    tpb.Phone = "555-555-555";
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = tpb;
                }
            }
            
        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);
    }

// function GetReturnAddresses() // returns the return address list or undefined on failure
function GetReturnAddresses()
	{
		var userMethodParams = { "action": "GetD2MAddressBook"};
		
		var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
		
		var returnAddressList = undefined;
		
		thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
			{
				alert(response.ErrorMessage);
			} 
			else 
			{
				
				var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data);
				returnAddressList = json.ReturnAddressList;		
				returnAddressList.forEach(function (returnAddress) {
					var x = returnAddress;
					console.log(x);
				});
			}
		});
		return returnAddressList;
	}
