// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {   
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); })
        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"], button[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"]', translateDates);
        $('a[href="/Manage"][title="Manage"]').remove();

        
        setInterval(function() {
            translateDates();
            $('button').each(function() {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let text = $(this).text().trim();
                let month = text.split(' ')[0];

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-info.uib-datepicker-current.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Today') {
                        $(this).text('Aujourd\'hui');  // Translate "Today" to French
                    }
                });
                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-danger.uib-clear.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Clear') {
                        $(this).text('Effacer');  // Translate "Clear" to French
                    }
                });

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-success.pull-right.uib-close.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Close') {
                        $(this).text('Fermer');  // Translate "Close" to French
                    }
                });
                
        
                for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                    if (month.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                        $(this).prop('disabled', true);  // Disable the button if it contains a month name
                        return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 1500);
       
         
        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
        
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }


            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }


            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

        var intervalId = setInterval(function() {
            client.init(); 
            clearInterval(intervalId);
        }, 1000);

        switch(location) {
            case '/shipping':
                this.vm.translations.ThinClient.CreateAShipment = "Créer un envoi";
                break;
            case '/history':
                $("h4:first").text("Historique");
                
                break;
            // Add more cases as needed
        }
     }

// RePrintAMP(Package) // returns void
function RePrintAMP(Package){
        let GlobalMSN = $(Package).data('custom-attribute1');
        let Carrier = $(Package).data('custom-attribute2');

        if(!Carrier.includes("CONNECTSHIP") && !Carrier.includes("TANDATA_LTL")){
          alert("Funcionality only support CONNECTSHIP carriers");
          return;
        }
        
        let Machine = '';
        fetch('https://localhost:5001/api/SystemInformation/ComputerName',{
            method:'GET',
        }).then(response => response.json())
        .then(data2 => {
            Machine = data2;
            CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN, Machine)
            
        }).catch(error => {
            console.log(error);
            CallUserMethod(GlobalMSN)
        });
    }

// function AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = GetShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
    function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);

            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        // check to make sure the user doesnt need supervisor permission
        var NoApprovalNeeded = [
            // services
            "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND",
            "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.3DA",
            "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD",
            "UPSAPI.UPS.GND",
            "UPSAPI.UPS.3DA",
            "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED",
            // payment terms
            "CONSIGNEE",
            "PREPURCHASED"
        ];

        // popup in place of email
        /*
        var supervisorEmail = callUserMethod(2);
        if (supervisorEmail != '') {
            supervisorEmail = ',' + supervisorEmail;
        }
        var requestorNotes = $("[property=MiscReference1] input").val();
        if (requestorNotes == "") {
            requestorNotes = "*Please be sure to update the requestor note setcion and provide some information supporting the shipment choices in your supervisor email";
        }
        var confirmMessage = "WARNING: This shipment will require Supervisor approval.\rPlease include the following information:\r" + requestorNotes + "\r\rSend your email to: \ralberto.pla@globaleagle.com,Ryan.Saladeen@globaleagle.com" + supervisorEmail +"\r\rClick OK to save or Cancel to make changes";
        */
           
        //message when email is in place
        var confirmMessage = "WARNING: This shipment will require Supervisor approval. \r\rClick OK to save and sent a notifications \rClick Cancel to make changes";

        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3 != "Approved") {
            if (callUserMethod(1) == "supervisor" || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ConsigneeThirdPartyBilling == true) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = "No Approval Required";
            } else {
                if (NoApprovalNeeded.includes(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol) ||
                    NoApprovalNeeded.includes(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms)) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = "No Approval Required";
                } else {
                    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference3 != "Approved") {
                        if (confirm(confirmMessage)) {
                            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = "Approval Required";
                            // set email variables
                            requestorEmail = $("[property=MiscReference12] input").val();
                            requestorNotes = $"[property=MiscReference1] input".val();
                            approverNotes = $("[property=MiscReference4] input").val();
                            // send the email
                            callUserMethod(3, requestorEmail, requestorNotes, approverNotes);
                            this.vm.saveShipment();
                        } 
                        throw ({ message: "Print process cancelled", errorCode: "NOTICE: " });
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// Success(msg) // returns undefined

                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                }

                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/') {
            var bmvar = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + "#!/batchmanager";
            window.location.replace(bmvar);
        }
        
        //<a href="" ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(batch.Info.BatchReference)" class="ng-binding">000046</a>
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/batchmanager') {
            var waitForT = setInterval(function () {
            //  $('body').delegate('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
            const alink = $('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(batch.Info.BatchReference)"]:visible');
            if (alink.length > 0)
            {
                $(alink).trigger('click');
                clearInterval(waitForT);
            }
            
                        // $('a[ng-click="vm.linkToDetails(0)"]').trigger('click');
                    // }); //end button delegate
        //}
            }, 250);
        }
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/batchdetail') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                try {
                    $('body').delegate('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var dueDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (dueDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');
                    
                    if (!$('#HazAlertShipment_panel').is(':visible')) {
	                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').modal('show');
	                $('#HazAlertShipment_panel').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
	                	$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
	                });
	            }
                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }
        
        if (window.location.hash == '#!/history') {
        }
        
        $('select[id="reports"]').hide();
        $('ul.navbar-nav a:contains("History")').text('Claim Search');
    } //end PageLoaded

// PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns undefined
    this.PreSearchHistory = function(searchCriteria) {
        var startShipdate = new Date();
        startShipdate.setDate(startShipdate.getDate() - 90);    
        this.vm.dtstart = startShipdate;
        searchCriteria.WhereClauses.filter(function (w) {
            if (w.FieldName == 'Shipdate' && w.Operator == 3) {
                w.FieldValue = startShipdate.toISOString().slice(0, 10);                
            }
        });
    }

// PostSearchHistory(packages) // returns undefined
    this.PostSearchHistory = function(packages) {
        //debugger;
        for (let i = 0; i < packages.length; i++)
        {
            const currentDate = new Date();
            currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate());
            
            const shipDate = new Date(packages[i].Shipdate.Year,packages[i].Shipdate.Month-1,packages[i].Shipdate.Day);
            //alert(packages[i].Shipdate.Year + " | " + packages[i].Shipdate.Month + " | " + packages[i].Shipdate.Day)
            //alert(shipDate)
            
            const diffTime = Math.abs(shipDate - currentDate);
            const diffDays = Math.floor(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)); 
            //console.log(diffTime + " milliseconds");
            //alert(diffDays + " days");
            if(diffDays > 30)
            {
                packages[i].CantPrint = true;
            }
        }
    }

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
		//alert("Country " + nameaddress.Country);
		
		var clientContext;
		var resp;

        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: "api/usercontext/GET",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {
                debugger;
                clientContext = result;
            },
            error: function (jqXhr, exception) {
                debugger;
            }
        });
     
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",           
            data: { UserContext: clientContext , "Data": nameaddress.Country},    
            success: function (response) {
                debugger;
				resp = JSON.stringify(response);
				resp = JSON.parse(resp);
				if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
				{
					var IOR = JSON.parse(resp.Data);
					shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ImporterOfRecord = IOR;
				}
				else
				{
					alert('No available Importer of Records');
				}
            },
            error: function (xhr) {
                debugger;
                alert(xhr.responseText);
            }
        });
		
	}

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        //getUserContext();  // Removed for CBR fix 07202022

        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// this.EmailNotificationAddress(event) // returns undefined
this.EmailNotificationAddress = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];
        debugger;
        // if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
        //     SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
        //     SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else {
        //     SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // }

        if (ngModelName == 'ShipNotificationEmail') {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    };

// function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail === undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() === '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g');
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail === undefined || pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail.trim() === '') {
                pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g')
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g')
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// ExportManifestData() // returns void
    function ExportManifestData()
    {   
		//var d = new Date();
		//var manifestdate = [d.getMonth()+1, d.getDate(), d.getFullYear()].join('/');	
		//debugger;
		var today = new Date();
		var dd = today.getDate();
		var mm = today.getMonth()+1; 
		var yyyy = today.getFullYear();
		
		if(dd<10) 
		{
			dd='0'+dd;
		} 

		if(mm<10) 
		{
			mm='0'+mm;
		} 		
		
		today = mm+'/'+dd+'/'+yyyy;
		
		var manifestdate = prompt("Enter the Ship Date to export (MM/DD/YYYY)", today);	
		
		//Check if Cancel Button was selected
		if (manifestdate === null) 
		{
			return; 
		}
		
		// I am adding a prefix to the beginging of the search value to know what code to run on the user method as this method is going to be used for other functions
        //var params = "manifestdataexport|" + manifestdate;
		
        var data = {
            'UserContext': client.userContext,
            'Data' : 'manifestdataexport|' + manifestdate
        }

        $.post({ 
            url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
            data,
            headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
        }).done(function (result) {
			//debugger;
			if (result != null && result != 'undefined' && result != '')
            {
                alert(result.Data);
            }
            else
            {
                alert("No data was returned from manifest data export call");
            } 
		}).fail(function (err) {
		    //debugger;
			//alert(e.message);
            alert("The process is taking longer than usual to complete but will continue to run on the server until all records are transferred");
		});	

        showDelayMessage();
    }

			dd='0'+dd;
		} 

		if(mm<10)

			mm='0'+mm;
		}

		{
			return; 
		}

// Source: L9 Sports (L9SPORTS)_L9 Client Rules_1694.cs
// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

       // alert("post");
       // alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        var addressName = new AddressEntry(nameaddress);
       //  alert("address name");
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = addressName.ToRef1;
       // alert(JSON.stringify(nameaddress));
    };

// Source: M&T Bank (MTBank)_MTBank_1506.cs
// getCostCenterReport(element) // returns the $.post promise when a cost center is present
function getCostCenterReport(element) {
    debugger;
    var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
    var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
    var context = client.userContext;
    var costcenter = $(element).attr('data-costcenter');
    if (costcenter) {
        var searchCriteria = { DateStart: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtstart"]').val(), DateEnd: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtend"]').val(), CostCenter: costcenter };
        var data = { Action: element.id, Content: JSON.stringify(searchCriteria) };
       return $.post({ url:shipExecServiceUrl +'/UserMethod',
              data: {UserContext: userContext, Data:JSON.stringify(data)}, headers: authorizationToken},
            function (response, status, xhr) {
                downloadFile(costcenter, response["Data"]);
            }
        ).done(function () {
        });
    }
}

// dismissDialog() // returns undefined
function dismissDialog() {
    $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
        $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
    })
}

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Inbound Returns CBR_CA_TO_US_2497.cs
// function setResponseLabel(responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) // returns undefined
    this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

// setUploadDelegates() // returns void
    function setUploadDelegates() {

        debugger;
        setCommodityDelegate();

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change');

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {

            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');

            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    debugger;
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {

                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            //var test = this.setResponseLabel;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click', function (e) {
            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsModalInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsModalInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsModalInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsModalInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";
            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabelModal = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
                if (uploadSuccessLabelModal) {
                    uploadSuccessLabelModal.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    var test2 = that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                }
                else {
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 2).then(function (ret) {
                        //debugger;

                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }


                    });
                }
            }
        });

    };

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Inbound Returns CBR_US_TO_US_2499.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //Storing the Number of Maximum labels in Misc Referene14.
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#Maxlabel').val();
        //Validating the maximum label count.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == "" || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 % 1 !== 0) {
            alert("Maximum label count is invalid");
            throw new Error("Maximum label count is invalid");
        }
        else if (!(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 >= 1 && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 <= 25)) {
            throw new Error("Number of labels needs to be a valid number between 1 and 25.");
        }

    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        //Declaring variables.
        var custom1_values, custom1, custom2, custom3, custom4, custom5, custom6, customData;
        var customValues = {};
        var customKeysArray = [];
        var CustomData_AfterCustom4 = [];
        var item;

        customData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        // Iterate over the CustomData array and map values to their respective keys
        $.each(customData, function (index, item) {
            customValues[item.Key] = item.Value;
        });

        if (this.vm.profile.Name == 'Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile') {
            for (var i in customData.length) {
                item = customData[i];
                customKeysArray.push(item.Key);
            }

            var startIndex = -1;
            // Find the index of the key "Custom5"
            for (var i = 0; i < customData.length; i++) {
                if (customData[i].Key === "Custom5") {
                    startIndex = i;
                    break;
                }
            }

            // If "Custom5" is found, start storing values from it onwards
            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                for (var j = startIndex; j < customData.length; j++) {
                    CustomData_AfterCustom4.push(customData[j].Value);
                }
            }

            // Now, customValues object contains all custom values accessible by their keys
            var custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            var custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
            var custom3 = customValues['Custom3'];
            var custom4 = customValues['Custom4'];
            var custom5 = customValues['Custom5'];
            var custom6 = customValues['Custom6'];
        } else {
            //debugger;
            custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
        }

        //Checking DryIceRequired sets true via User Custom1 data.
        if (custom1.split(',').length > 1) {
            custom1_values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom1, ',');
        } else {
            throw new Error("Custom1 is not Comma delimited string.");
        }

        //Setting the Leg1Shipper
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = custom1_values[0];

        //Creating Dry Ice Required Checkbox
        if ($('#DryIceRequired').length == 0 && custom1_values[1] == "true") {
            //Adding DryIceRequired checkbox and its label.
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<input />', {
                type: 'checkbox',
                id: 'DryIceRequired',
                name: 'DryIceRequired'
            }));
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<label />', {
                for: 'DryIceRequired',
                text: 'Dry Ice Required'
            }));
        }

        //Comparing the User Custom2 with the Profile enabled Services and remove the unmatched services from the Service UI.
        var arrayValues_custom2;
        if (custom2 != null || custom2 != undefined) {
            arrayValues_custom2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom2, ',');
            var matchedValues = [];
            var profileServices = this.vm.profile.Services;
            profileServices.forEach(function (value1) {
                var serviceExists = arrayValues_custom2.some(function (value) {
                    return value1.Name.indexOf(value) !== -1;
                });
                if (serviceExists) {
                    matchedValues.push(value1);
                }
            });

            //Populating the Matched services on the Service UI.
            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mySelect = $('select[multiple="multiple"][property="Service"]');
                mySelect.empty(); //Clearing the existing Services listed out in the Service UI list.

                for (var i in matchedValues) {
                    mySelect.append($('<option></option>').attr('value', matchedValues[i].Symbol).text(matchedValues[i].Name));

                }
            });
        }

        //Retrieving Custom Data values after CustomData4(Leg2 Companies).
        var CustomDataCount = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length;

        var CustomData_FirstValues = []; //Fetch the First strings from Customdata after Custom4.
        var CustomData_OtherValues = []; //Fetch the rest of other strings from Customdata after Custom4.

        // Loop through each inner array in CustomData_AfterCustom4
        for (var i = 0; i < CustomData_AfterCustom4.length; i++) {

            var customData = CustomData_AfterCustom4[i];

            //var customData_values = customData.Value;

            var valuesArray = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(customData, ',');

            var firstValue = valuesArray.shift().trim();

            //Store the first string from the Custom data.
            CustomData_FirstValues.push(firstValue);

            //Store the remaining values
            CustomData_OtherValues.push(valuesArray.map(val => val.trim()));
        }


        //debugger;
        //Enabling the MiscReference1 field based on Profile.
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {

           // debugger;

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";
                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').hide();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').hide();
                }
                else {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').show();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').show();
                }

            });

            //Creating Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox
            if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').length == 0 && custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                    $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                        'type': 'checkbox',
                        'id': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn',
                        'name': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn'
                    }),
                    $('<label />').attr('for', 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').text('Central Labs Frozen Samples Return')
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);

            }
            else {
                //Creating Empty Packaging Checkbox
                if ($('#EmptyPackaging').length == 0) {
                    //debugger;
                    var checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                        $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                            'type': 'checkbox',
                            'id': 'EmptyPackaging',
                            'name': 'EmptyPackaging'
                        }),
                        $('<label />').attr('for', 'EmptyPackaging').text('Empty Packaging')
                    );

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty);

                }



                //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Empty Packaging Checkbox is checked.
                $('body').delegate('#EmptyPackaging', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#EmptyPackaging').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "true";
                    } else {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "false";
                    }
                });
            }


            //Setting Leg2 Dry Ice weight hidden by default
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
            });
            //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox is checked.
            $('body').delegate('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn', 'change', function (e) {
                if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').is(':checked')) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "true";

                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').show();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').show();

                } else {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "false";
                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
                }
            });

            //Creating Leg2 Dry Ice Weight
            if ($('#Leg2DryIceWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:120px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Dry Ice Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:140px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }

            //Setting MiscReference10 to true if Leg2 Dry Ice Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2DryIceWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10 = $(this).val();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });
        
    }

// PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) // returns void
    function PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) {
        debugger;

        var jsonData;

        var dataObject = {
            ConsolidationTrackingNumber: docboxtrackingNumber,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);

        debugger;

        var data = {
            Data: payload,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        // Show the spinner
        $("#loadingSpinner").show();

        var ajaxRequest = clientService1.thinclientService1APIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);

        ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
            jsonData = data.Data;
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            console.log(jsonData);
            setTimeout(function () {
                debugger;
                var dataObj = JSON.parse(jsonData.replaceAll('&quot;', '"'));
                var htmlString = '<div>Total Invoice Amount: '
                    + dataObj.Total
                    + ' '
                    + dataObj.TotalUOM
                    + '<br /><hr />';
                var i = 0, len = dataObj.TrackingNumbers.length;
                for (; i < len; i++) {
                    var currentTracking = dataObj.TrackingNumbers[i];
                    var itemString = currentTracking.TrackingNumber
                    htmlString += itemString + "<br />";
                }
                htmlString += '</div>';
                $('#infoModalLabel').html(htmlString);
                $('#infoModal').modal('show');

            }, 50);
        }).fail(function (xhr, status, error) {
            console.error("Error:", error);
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            alert("Failed to get data.");

        }).always(function () {
            // Hide the spinner regardless of success or failure
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
        });
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
         }
 
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;
        
        
            $(document).ready(function() {
               
             $("#OK").on("click", function() {
            
                 var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if(arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)){
                     var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue); 
                     var selectedStudy= arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                     //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                     
                     var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                     var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                      shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                      
                     var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                     var selectedSite= arrayOrders2[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                }
                else
                 {
                     alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                     throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                 }
        
                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                 GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);
                
                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                
            });
        
        });
     
    }

// Source: MarkenLLP2 (MLLP2)_Inbound Returns CBR_EU_TO_UK_1916.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
          debugger;
        //If the user profile is EU to UK, then Pickup LatestTimeReady can be calculated.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 == "2") {
          
            var MiscRef10 = formatNumberToTime(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10);

            // Split the times into hours and minutes
            var parts1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9.split(":");
            var parts2 = MiscRef10.split(":");

            // Parse the hours and minutes as integers
            var hours1 = parseInt(parts1[0], 10);
            var minutes1 = parseInt(parts1[1], 10);
            var hours2 = parseInt(parts2[0], 10);
            var minutes2 = parseInt(parts2[1], 10);

            // Add the hours and minutes together
            var totalHours = hours1 + hours2;
            var totalMinutes = minutes1 + minutes2;

            // Handle carryover from minutes to hours
            if (totalMinutes >= 60) {
                totalHours += Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);
                totalMinutes %= 60;
            }

            // Format the result as "hh:mm"
            var result = totalHours.toString().padStart(2, '0') + ':' + totalMinutes.toString().padStart(2, '0');

            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = result;
            
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 > shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12) 
                {
                alert("Calculated Pickup Latest Time Ready is later than the Maximum Pickup Latest Time Ready for the user.");
                throw new Error("Calculated Pickup Latest Time Ready is later than the Maximum Pickup Latest Time Ready for the user.");
                }

             //Format the number to HH:MM    
             function formatNumberToTime(number) {
            
                            if (number < 0 || number > 23) {
                                return "Invalid hour";
                            }
                            // Use String interpolation to format the number as "X:00"
                            return `${number}:00`;
                        }
                        
                        
            $('[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]').trigger('click');
            // Assigning the Pickup request properties.
            this.vm.pickup.ContactName = $('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Contact"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.ContactPhone = $('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Phone"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.PaymentType = "PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT";
            this.vm.pickup.EarliestTimeReady = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference9"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.LatestTimeReady = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11;

            if (this.vm.pickup != null) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    $('[ng-click="vm.ok()"]') .trigger('click');
                }, 100);
            }
        }

this.PageLoaded = function (location) {  
        if(window.location.hash == "#!/shipping")
        {

            {
                if(window.jQuery)
                {
                    /* Stop the timer */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                     $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) { $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide(); });
                }
            },50);
        }    
    }
