// Source: Memorial Sloan-Kettering Cancer Center  (MSKCC)_MSKCC_Reference_Rules_63.cs
// AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
    function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

    function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {

                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');

// getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) // returns an object containing Consignee and/or Origin email addresses
    function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

// client.alert() // returns an object with Info, Success, and Danger alert display methods
alert: (function () {
            var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
            var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
            uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

            $('body').append(uibalert);
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

            return {
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }
            }
        })(),

// client.dismiss() // returns an object with All, Info, Success, and Danger alert dismissal methods
dismiss: (function () {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { client.dismiss.Danger() });
            return {
                All: function () { $('div[role="alert"]').hide() },
                Info: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-info:visible').hide() },
                Success: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-success:visible').hide() },
                Danger: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-danger:visible').hide() }
            }
        })(),

// Source: MGMResorts (MGMRESOR)_Outbound Client Rules_1649.cs
// showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) // returns undefined
function showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) {
        //debugger;
        // hide loading spinner
        toggleDownloadLoading(false, option);
        decodeReturnString(response);

        thisRef.AlertTitle = title;
        if (response.ErrorCode == 0) {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.Data;
        } else {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.ErrorMessage;
        }
        // setting dom values since ng-model isn't available
        var responseText = response.ErrorCode == 0 || !response.ErrorMessage  ? response.Data : response.ErrorMessage
        alertModal.find('h4').text(title);
        alertModal.find('p').text(responseText);
        alertModal.modal('show');
    }

// decodeReturnString(data) // returns data
function decodeReturnString(data) {
        try {
            data.Data = $('<div />').html(data.Data).text();
            if (data.ErrorMessage) {
                data.ErrorMessage = $('<div />').html(data.ErrorMessage).text();
            }
            return data;
        }
        catch (error) {
            console.log(error);
            //console.log(data);
        }
    }

// Source: Mimaki USA (MIMAKI)_Mimaki CBR_2455.cs
// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

// Source: NAGINA INTERNATIONAL (NAGINA)_ISMEA_FTP_1585.cs
// function getFTPUploaded() // returns undefined
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Nexus (NEXUS)_Nexus CBR 2.3 Fix_1760.cs
// GetAddressBook(addressBookName, context) // returns an address book object or undefined
    this.GetAddressBook = function (addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false);
        if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
            client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
        } else {
            if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                client.alert.Danger('Address Book: "' + addressBookName + '" does not exist');                
            } else {
                return response.AddressBooks[0];
            }
        }
    }

// GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, context, codeReference) // returns an address book entries array or undefined
    this.GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBook, context, codeReference) {
        if (addressBook != undefined) {
            var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: codeReference, Operator: 0 }] };
            var data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBook.Id], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } else {
                if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                    client.alert.Danger('Address Book Entries: No address found in "' + addressBookName + '" address book');
                } else {
                    return response.AddressBookEntries;
                }
            }
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //Setting the return address on Dicks Sporting Goods orders to their address
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 == "8778469997")
        {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Company = "Dicks Sporting Goods";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Contact = "";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address1 = "1314 Conklin Rd.";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address2 = "STE B";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.City = "Conklin";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.StateProvince = "NY";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.PostalCode = "13748";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Country = "US";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Phone = "8778469997";
        }
        
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms == "CONSIGNEE")
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').focus();
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 == "RTGD")
        {
            alert("Please ensure to rate and select the desired service for shipping.");
        }
    }

        }
    }

// alert.Success(msg) // returns void
Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 !== "undefined") 
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "";
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

function GetPreAlert(element, context) {

		var group = JSON.parse(jsonGroup);

		var data = {
			UserContext: client.userContext,
			Data: "GetPreAlert" + jsonGroup
		}

	}

// function sendPreAlertApi(method, data, isAsync) // returns the jQuery post request
function sendPreAlertApi(method, data, isAsync) {
		var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
		var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
		return $.post({
				url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method,
				data: data,
				async: isAsync,
				headers: authorizationToken,
				datatype: 'blob'
			},
			function(response, status, xhr) {
				var preAlertObject = ParseReturnData(response["Data"])
				const byteArr = base64ToArrayBuffer(preAlertObject.DataFile);
				saveByteArray(preAlertObject.FileName, byteArr);
			},
		).done(function() {});
	}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
    if(location === "/")
     document.location = "#!/shipping";
     
    if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") 
    {
      var checkExist = setInterval(function() 
      {
          if (window.jQuery) 
          {
              /* Stop the timer. */
              clearInterval(checkExist);
              $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) { $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide(); });
            }
          }, 50);
      }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;        
        //$.get({ url: "http://localhost:9091/api/websites/96659", cache: false })
        //    .fail(function (e) {
        //        alert('The Scale Service may not be running. Please check to make sure the ShipExec Client Service is running');
        //    });
        //}
     
        if(scale == 'EC')   {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: "http://localhost:9093/api/websites/96659",
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                success: function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    //alert(result);
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5= result;
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7= "EC";                       
                },
                error: function(jqXhr, exception) {
                alert("Please check the Express Cube Scale Service to make sure the service is running " + exception);                    
                }
            });
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;                        

        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 == 'YES' ) {
                shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "ShipExec Alert";
                shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference + " has previously shipped today " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ShipDate +  ". Click Yes to ship again. Click No to abort.";
                angular.element('[ng-model="AlertModal"]').modal('show');
            }
        }
        
        if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== null)              {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 !== 'ADDRESS1MATCH' ) {
                //alert("The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package");
                this.vm.alerts = [{type:'danger', msg:'The Address Line 1 was not matched. Please run Address Validation prior to shipping this package'}];
            }   
        }
    }

// Source: PRA Developer (PRADeveloper)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1523.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// EmailNotificationAddress(event) // returns undefined
this.EmailNotificationAddress = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];
        debugger;
        // if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
        //     SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
        //     SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else {
        //     SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // }

        if (ngModelName == 'ShipNotificationEmail') {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    };

// SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail === undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() === '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g');
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail === undefined || pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail.trim() === '') {
                pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g');
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail === undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() === '') {
                pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress;
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress, 'g');
            notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) {
        /* This enables the button to edit the Third Party Billing Information. */
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', false).attr('disabled', false);

        /* Check the box for Third Party Billing which will bring up the modal.  Fill the modal with values.  Click Save. */
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', true).attr('checked', true).change();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {}
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = 'PRA Global';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = '995 Research Park Blvd';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = 'Suite 300';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = 'Charlottesville';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = 'VA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = '22911';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = '883F79';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = 'US'
    }

// DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() // returns undefined
function DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() {
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', false).attr('checked', false);
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);
    }

// Source: Purolator (PURT)_PurolatorUserMethod_1914.cs
// customUserMethod() // returns void
    function customUserMethod () {
        debugger;
        var dateSelected = $('#exportDate').val();
        var shipper = $('#gateway :selected').text();
        var carrier = $('#carrier :selected').text();
        
        if (carrier === 'UPS')
        {
            carrier = 'CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS';
        }
        else
        {
            carrier = 'CONNECTSHIP_DHLXMLPI.DHL';
        }

        var data = { DateSelected: dateSelected, Shipper: shipper, Carrier: carrier};
        var payload = { UserContext: client.userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) };
        var result = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', payload, false).responseJSON;
        
        debugger;
        if (result.ErrorCode > 0 || result == undefined) {
            client.alert.Danger(result.ErrorCode + ': ' + result.ErrorMessage);
        } else if (result.Message != undefined || result.Message != "") {
            client.alert.Success(result.Message);
        } else {
            client.alert.Success(result.Message);
        }
    }

// Source: R.BCC EXPORTERS PRIVATE LIMITED (R.BCC)_ISMEA_FTP_1716.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Rainier Arms (RNRARMS)_RainierArms shipping CBR_1640.cs
// PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
	};

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0)
		{
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = false;    // signature_required_checkbox
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = true;    // autoship_checkbox
	};

// downloadFromCin7API() // returns void
    this.downloadFromCin7API = function() {
		//debugger;
		let data = { Action: 'Download_Orders', Params: ''};
		
		downloadOrders = true;
		toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);

		// call SBR UserMethod to access Cin7 API to download orders
		$.post({
			url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
			data: {
			    UserContext: client.userContext,
			    Data: JSON.stringify(data)
			}
		}).done(function (data) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
		    
			if (data.Data === true) {
				alert('Download successful!');
			}
			else {
				alert('Download was not successful');
			}
		}).fail(function (err) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
		    console.log(err.responseJSON);
			alert('Download was not successful');

// Source: Rite Kem (RITEKEM)_RiteKem_1637.cs
// getHazmatReport() // returns the result of a POST request when a shipper is selected, otherwise undefined
function getHazmatReport() {
        debugger;
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        var context = client.userContext;
        var shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedShipper"] option:selected').val();
        if (shipper) {
            var searchCriteria = { DateStart: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtstart"]').val(), DateEnd: $('input[ng-model="vm.dtend"]').val(), Shipper: shipper };
            var data = { Action: "HazmatReport", Content: JSON.stringify(searchCriteria) };
           return $.post({ url:shipExecServiceUrl +'/UserMethod',
                  data: {UserContext: client.userContext, Data:JSON.stringify(data)}, headers: authorizationToken},
                function (response, status, xhr) {
                    downloadFile(shipper, response["Data"]);
                }
            ).done(function () {
            });
        }
    }

// downloadFile(exportFileName, encodedString) // returns undefined
function downloadFile(exportFileName, encodedString) {
        var decodedResult = atob(encodedString); // decode a base-64 encoded string
        var csvFile = new Blob([decodedResult], { type: "text/csv" });
    
        var ie = navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE\s([\d.]+)/),
            ie11 = navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7.0/) && navigator.userAgent.match(/rv:11/),
            ieEdge = navigator.userAgent.match(/Edge/g),
            ieVer = (ie ? ie[1] : (ie11 ? 11 : (ieEdge ? 12 : -1)));
    
        exportFileName = exportFileName + '.csv';
    
        if (ieVer > -1) {
            window.navigator.msSaveBlob(csvFile, exportFileName);
    
        } else {
            var downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
            downloadLink.download = exportFileName;
            downloadLink.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(csvFile);
            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
            downloadLink.click();
            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
        }
    }

// Source: Sazerac (Sazerac)_Sazerac CBR_1680.cs
// openFileDialog() // returns undefined
function openFileDialog() {
        //debugger;
        var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader");

        if (filesSelected !== undefined) {
            const fileReader = new FileReader();

            if (filesSelected.files[0]) {
                fileReader.readAsDataURL(filesSelected.files[0]);
            }

            fileReader.onload = function (event) {
                var files = event.target.result;

                // Get base64 file data
                var contents = event.target.result.split(',')[1];

                // adding prefix to beginning of file data to send to user method
                var fileData = "file|" + contents;

                // $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                // {
                //     UserContext: userContext,
                //     Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)

                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    // result.Data should be unencoded [Success] or [Error] string
                    if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1) {
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                    else {
                        // display error
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            };
        }
    }

// ParseJson(result) // returns undefined
function ParseJson(result) {
        //debugger;
        var jsonLoad = result; //jQuery.parseJSON(result);
       
        if (jsonLoad !== null && jsonLoad !== undefined)
        {
            $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    
            //#region Build Drop-Down List
            var html = "";

            for (let i in jsonLoad.listData)
            {
                html += "<option value='" + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "'>" + jsonLoad.listData[i].fullName + " " + jsonLoad.listData[i].glCode + "</option>";
            }
    
            if (jsonLoad.listData.length === 0)
            {
                alert("No records were returned from search")
            }
            else //More than one record returned
            {
                //$("#costcodes").remove();
                //$(html).insertAfter("#searchButton");
                $("#costcodes").append(html);
                $('#costcodes').change(function() {
                    populateShipExec();
                });
                $("#costcodes").show();
            }
    
        }
        else
        {
            alert("Error populating dropdown box --- " + jsonLoad.ErrorMessage);
        }
    
    }

// populateShipExec() // returns undefined
function populateShipExec() {
        //Get cost code value from selected value in drop down list
        var costcode = document.getElementById('costcodes').value;
        var fullitemtext = document.getElementById('costcodes').options[document.getElementById('costcodes').selectedIndex].text;
    
        //Populate Cost Code in shipper_reference field
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].ShipperReference = costcode;
    
        //Populate Full Value in Reference Field 3
        vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference3 = fullitemtext;
    
        //Reset ShipExec Controls
        //document.getElementById('costcodes').outerHTML = "";
        $('#costcodes').off('change');
        $('#costcodes option:not(:first)').remove();
        $('#costcodes').hide();
        ////resetShipExec();
        $('#search_input').val('');
        $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        var shipperSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper;

        //Skip Ship Goods Type Selection for these international shipper origins
        if (shipperSymbol != "SEGONZAC_FR" && shipperSymbol != "SURREY_UK" && shipperSymbol != "DUBLIN_IE" && shipperSymbol != "NAYANDA_IN" && shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            var shipGoodsType = document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').options[document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').selectedIndex].value;
            var pkg1MiscRef4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
            //if (shipGoodsType == null || shipGoodsType == 'undefined' || shipGoodsType == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default')
            if (pkg1MiscRef4 == null || pkg1MiscRef4 == undefined || pkg1MiscRef4 == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default') {
                $("#ship_goods_type").val('default');
                //$('#ship_goods_type').css('background-color', '#FF3333');
                $('#ship_goods_type').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Shipment Goods Type on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
                return;
            }
        }

        //#region Require Field Validation
        if (shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            //debugger;
            //var costCodeValue = $("#ctl00_cphContent_right_tabs_ref_tab_ref_ctrl_misc_ref_pane_content_misc_reference_3_txt").val();
            var costCodeValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
            if (costCodeValue == null || costCodeValue == undefined || costCodeValue == '') {
                $('#costcodes').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Cost Code value on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
            }
        }
        //#endregion

        var thirdParty = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19;
        var adultSignature = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20;

        userParams.third_party_rule = thirdParty;
        userParams.adult_signature_required_rule = adultSignature;
    };

// Source: Soundoff Signal (SOS)_Warehouse Shipping CBR_1803.cs
// UpdateToastNotification(MsgObject, Callback) // returns void
  UpdateToastNotification = (MsgObject, Callback) =>
  {
    const attr = (MsgObject.Action == 'Error' ? 'Error' : 'Success');

    const icons = {
      'AddItem': 'glyphicon-plus-sign',
      'AddContainer': 'glyphicon-plus-sign',
      'RemoveItem': 'glyphicon-minus-sign',
      'RemoveContainer': 'glyphicon-minus-sign',
      'EditHarmonizedData': 'glyphicon-edit',
      'CloseContainer': 'glyphicon-folder-close',
      'SaveShipment': 'glyphicon-save',
      'Error': 'glyphicon-alert'
    };

    let toast = $('div.toast').first();
    $(toast).attr('msg', 'Default');

    let header = $(toast).find('.msg-header').first();
    let msg = $(toast).find('.msg-text').first();

    let i = $(toast).find('i').removeClass((index, className) => { return (className.match(/(^|\s)glyphicon-\S+/g) || []).join(' '); });
    $(i).addClass(icons[MsgObject.Action]);

    if (!$(toast).is(':visible')) { $(toast).fadeIn(); }

    $(msg).html(new DynamicHtml().GetNewToastMessage(MsgObject));

    $(header).text(attr);

    let a = 0;
    const inv = window.setInterval(() =>
    {
      a++;

      (a % 2 == 0 ? $(toast).attr('msg', 'Default') : $(toast).attr('msg', attr));

      if (a >= 7 && !$(toast).attr('Default'))
      {
        window.clearInterval(inv);
        return false;
      }

    }, 150);

    if (Callback && $.isFunction(Callback)) Callback();
  }

// function PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) 
    {        
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            var aTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            var searchText = "Email";
            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
                    if (aTags[i].textContent == searchText) {
                        var loaded = aTags[i];
                        aTags[i].click();
                    }
                }
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
                }
            }, 50); 
        }
        
           if (location === '/batchmanager') {
            $( "#btnCreateNewBatches" ).click(function() {                
                var userMethodParams = { "action": "CreateNewBatchForProcessing"};
            
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
                var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    alert("Batch creation request sent");
                }
            });

            var batchId = $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text();
            
            if(batchId !== null && batchId !== '')
            {
                var proceedToSetBatchPrinted = confirm("Confirm to set batch" + batchId + " as deleted? Click OK to continue or Cancel");
                
                if(proceedToSetBatchPrinted)
                {
                    var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetBatchAsPrinted", "batchid" : $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text()};
        
                    var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
        
                    var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
        
                    if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
                    {
                        client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
                    } 
                    else 
                    {
                        alert(batchId + " was set to deleted");
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert("No batch has been selected");
            }
            }); // end function
        }
    }

                }

            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");

                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();

        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// function client.alert // returns object with Info, Success, and Danger methods
    var client = {
        userContext: function () {
            var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
            var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
                var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
                userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
            }
            var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
            return $.get({url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
        }(),
        dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }),
        alert: (function () {
            var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
            var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
            uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

            $('body').append(uibalert);
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

            return {
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }
            }
        })()
    }

// function(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
          var employeeID;
          var BU;
          var OU;
          var CR;
          var locationCode;
         var CustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
            for (var Custom in CustomData) {
                     if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom1") employeeID = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                      if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom2") BU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
             
         if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
            alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
            if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
                  alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
                  shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;

// function getFTPUploaded() // returns undefined
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Tailor Made Compounding (TMC)_TailorMadeCompoundingClientTemplate_1691.cs
// ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities) // returns boolean indicating whether the consolidated opportunities value is valid
function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities)
    {
        var rexVal = /^[A-Z0-9]+((,|-)[A-Z0-9]+)*[A-Z0-9]+$/;
        var result = true;
        if (!rexVal.test(consolidatedOpportunities.toUpperCase()))
        {
            if (consolidatedOpportunities.trim()==="")
            {
                result=true;
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Consolidated opportunities not well formed.");
                result= false;
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

// Source: Target (TARGET)_Target CBR_2489.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; throws validation error when MiscReference1 is missing
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
        if (!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1.trim() === '') {
            // Highlight the field if it has no value
            waitForInputs();    

            const err = new Error('MiscReference1 is required');
            err.name = 'ValidationError'; // Optional custom name
            err.code = 'MISC_REF_001';    // Custom property
            throw err;
        } else {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model*="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.style.border = null;
                });
            }
        }

        function waitForInputs() {
            const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model$="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                input.style.border = '1px solid red';
                });
                observer.disconnect(); // stop watchin
            }
            });

            observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });

        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined; clears field highlighting for MiscReference1
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model*="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.style.border = null;
                });
            }
    }

// sendPreAlertApi(method, data, isAsync) // returns jQuery promise/XHR response
    function sendPreAlertApi (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken },
                function (response, status, xhr) {
                    var preAlertObject = ParseReturnData(response["Data"])
                    downloadFile(preAlertObject.FileName, preAlertObject.DataFile);
                }
        ).done(function () {
            });
    }

// Info(msg) // returns undefined
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },

// Success(msg) // returns undefined
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },

// Danger(msg) // returns undefined
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined; may throw an error
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// dismissAlertDialog() // returns void
    function dismissAlertDialog() {

            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;
        //shipmentRequest.CreateShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User", shipmentRequest);
    };

    this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };
    
    this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
        var selectedValue = $('select[id="reports"]:eq(0)').val();
        var selectedReport = $("select[id='reports'] option[value='" + selectedValue + "'");
        //debugger;
        if(selectedReport[0].innerText !=="All History"){
            searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 0 });
        }
    }; 
        this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
            var customData = nameaddress.CustomData;
            var fieldName = "Custom2"
        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = customField.Value;
        });
        }
             
            if(nameaddress.Code == "hSTI-GLENALLEN")
            {
                glenallenShipment=true;
                var service = [{Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.NDA", Name: "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)"}];
                vm.profile.ProfileSetting.ServiceSelectionMode = 1;
                this.vm.selectedServices = service;
                this.vm.showServiceSelection=false;
            } 
    };

    function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        debugger;
         //  userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
         userContext = client.userContext;
    }

var clientService = {
    config: $.getJSON({url:'config.json', async: false}).responseJSON,
    authorizationToken: function () {
        if (JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")))
            return { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token };
    }
}

var client = {
    userContext: function () {
        var userContextUrl = 'api/usercontext/GET';
        var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        if (shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http')) {
            var url = new URL(shipExecServiceUrl);
            userContextUrl = url.origin + '/' + userContextUrl;
        }
        var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
        return $.get({url: userContextUrl, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
    }(),
    dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }),
    alert: (function () {
        var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
        var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
        uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

        $('body').append(uibalert);
        closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

        return {
            Info: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
            },
            Success: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
            },
            Danger: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
            }
        }
    })()
}

function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}
     function getUserName() {
        var helloUser = $('a[title="Manage"]:contains("Hello")').text();
        return helloUser.match(/[a-zA-Z]+[a-zA-Z0-9._]+@[a-zA-Z]+\.[a-zA-Z.]{2,5}/i)[0];
    }
}

// client.alert // returns object with Info(msg), Success(msg), and Danger(msg) functions for displaying alerts
    alert: (function () {
        var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
        var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
        uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

        $('body').append(uibalert);
        closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

        return {
            Info: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
            },
            Success: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
            },
            Danger: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
            }
        }
    })()

// validationCVIS(Type) // returns undefined
    function validationCVIS(Type){
        var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
        if(Shipper === "0"){
            client.alert.Danger("Select a valid Shipper");
        }else{
            var TrailerSortCode = $("#TrailerSortCode").val();
            if(TrailerSortCode === ""){
                client.alert.Danger("No Trailer Sort Code found for Shipper "+ Shipper);
            }else{
                //AllGood
                execCvisAction(Type);
            }
        }
       
    }

    function getShippersByProfile(){
	    var usermethodParams = { "action": 5, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":""};
	    var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
		var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
				client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
			} else {
				var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data); //$.parseJSON($("<div />").html(response.Data).text());//$.parseJSON(response.Data);
                $.each(json.Shippers, function (i, item) {
                    $('#CVIS_Shippers').append($('<option>', { 
                        value: item["value"],

			}
		});

    function getTrailerSortCodeByShipper(){
        var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
        if(Shipper != "0"){
            var usermethodParams = { "action": 6, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":Shipper};
			var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
        	var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
				if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
					client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
				} else {
					$("#TrailerSortCode").val(response.Data);
				}
			});
