// execCvisAction(Type) // returns undefined
    function execCvisAction(Type){
	    if(Type === "Add"){
			var TrailerNumber = $("#TrailerNumber").val();
			if(TrailerNumber === ""){
				client.alert.Danger("No Trailer Number provided");
			}else{
				var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
				var usermethodParams = { "action": 7, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":TrailerNumber, "shipper":Shipper};
				
				var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						client.alert.Success(response.Data);
					}
				});
			}
			/*$.ajax({
            type: "POST",
                url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                dataType: "json",
                data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
                success: function(response) {
                    alert(response.Data);
                },
                error: function (error) {
                    alert(error);
                }
            });*/
            
	    }
	    if(Type === "Close"){
	        if($('#UPSPackageCarPickup').is(":checked")){
	            var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
    	        var TrailerNumber = $("#TrailerNumber").val();
                var usermethodParams = { "action": 9, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":TrailerNumber, "shipper":Shipper};
            	var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						client.alert.Success(response.Data);
                        getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                        $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
					}
				});
				
				/*$.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                    url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
                    async: false,
                    cache: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
                    success: function(response) {
                        alert(response.Data);
                        if(response.Data === "Success"){
                            getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                            $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
                        }
                        
                    },
                    error: function (error) {
                        alert(error);
                    }
                });*/
	        }else{
	            var TrailerNumber = $("#TrailerNumber").val();
	            if(TrailerNumber === ""){
                    client.alert.Danger("No Trailer Number provided");
                }else{
                    //AllGood
                    OpenModalClose();
                }
	            
	            
	        }
	        
	    }
	}

// CloseReal() // returns undefined
    function CloseReal(){
	    var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
        var TrailerNumber = $("#TrailerNumber").val();
		var percentageComplete = $("#percentageComplete").val();
		if(percentageComplete === null || percentageComplete === ""){
		    client.alert.Danger("Percentage Complete is required")
		    return;
		}
        var usermethodParams = { "action": 8, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":percentageComplete, "trailerNumber":TrailerNumber, "shipper":Shipper};
    	
		var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
		var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
				client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
			} else {
				client.alert.Info(response.Data);
                if(response.Data === "Success"){
                    CloseModalClose();
                    getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                    $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
                }
			}
		});
		
		/*$.ajax({
        type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",
            data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
            success: function(response) {
                alert(response.Data);
                if(response.Data === "Success"){
                    CloseModalClose();
                    getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                    $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
                }
                
            },
            error: function (error) {
                alert(error);
            }
        });*/
	}

// UserMethod(logoNumber) // returns undefined
    function UserMethod(logoNumber) {

		if (logoNumber == 4) {

			var orderNumber = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();

			if (orderNumber === undefined || orderNumber === null || orderNumber === "") {

				client.alert.Danger("Missing or invalid Order Number, no update made.  Please enter a valid order number and try again.");
			}
			else {
			
				var usermethodParams = { "action": 4, "orderNumber": orderNumber, "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":""};
				var results;
				var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						results = response["Data"];
					}
				});
				
				
				/*$.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
                    async: false,
                    cache: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
                    success: function(response) {
                        results = response["Data"];
                        ;
                    },
                    error: function (error) {
                        alert("Finalize Shipment has failed, no update made to the system.  Contact Support.");
                    }
                });*/
			}
		}
		else {

			$("#fileLoader").click();

			var encodedBase64Logo;

			var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader").files;

			if (filesSelected.length > 0) {
				var fileToLoad = filesSelected[0];

				var fileReader = new FileReader();

				fileReader.readAsDataURL(fileToLoad);

				fileReader.onload = function (event) {
					var encodedBase64Logo = logoNumber + event.target.result;

					SoxOnWcfDblHop.userMethod(encodedBase64Logo,
						function (result) {
							// Do something with the data

							DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result);

						},
						function (e) {
							// Do something with the error

							alert(e.message);
						});
				};
			}
		}
	}

// DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result) // returns undefined
    function DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result) {

		var jsonLoad = jQuery.parseJSON(result);

		if (jsonLoad.logosuccess != null && jsonLoad.logosuccess != undefined) {

			if (jsonLoad.logosuccess != undefined) {
				alert(jsonLoad.logosuccess);
			}
			else {
				alert("There was an error attempting to save file to server.  File NOT updated, please try again.");
			}
		}
		else {

			if (jsonLoad != undefined && jsonLoad.error != null && jsonLoad.error != undefined) {
				alert(jsonLoad.error);
			}
			else {
				alert("There was an error attempting to save file to server.  File NOT updated, please try again.");
			}
		}
	}

// Source: VSP (VSP)_VSP Reference Rules 2.0_2445.cs
// client.alert // returns an object with Info(msg), Success(msg), and Danger(msg) methods
        alert: (function () {
            var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
            var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
            uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

            $('body').append(uibalert);
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

            return {
                Info: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
                },
                Success: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
                },
                Danger: function (msg) {
                    uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                    uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                    uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
                }
            }
        })()

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        GetUserContext();
        
        if(location=="/")
        {
        var welcomeExist = setInterval(function() {
           var welcome =  $('h1:contains("Welcome")');
            if (welcome.length)
            {
                clearInterval(welcomeExist);
                welcome.text("VW / Audi Versandportal");
            }
             
         }, 50); 
        
        
        var SystemExist = setInterval(function() {
           var SystemN =  $('h2:contains("System")');
            if (SystemN.length)
            {
                clearInterval(SystemExist);
                SystemN.text("Systembenachrichtigungen");
            }
             
         }, 50); 
        
        var CompanyExist = setInterval(function() {
           var CompanyN =  $('h2:contains("Company")');
            if (CompanyN.length)
            {
                clearInterval(CompanyExist);
                CompanyN.text("Unternehmensnachrichten");
            }
             
         }, 50); 
         
        var SiteExist = setInterval(function() {
           var SiteN =  $('h2:contains("Site")');
            if (SiteN.length)
            {
                clearInterval(SiteExist);
                SiteN.text("Seitenbenachrichtigung");
            }
             
         }, 50); 
            
        }
        
        var checkExist = setInterval(function() {
            if (window.jQuery)
            {
                /* Stop the timer. */
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('a:contains("Log off")').text("Abmelden");
                $('li a:contains("Shipping and Rating")').text("Versandbearbeitung");
                $('li a:contains("Shipping")').text("Versand");
                $('li a:contains("History")').text("Versandarchiv");
                $('li a:contains("Address Book")').text("Adressbuch");
            }
         }, 50); 
         
    };

                 this.GetWeight();

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        // default phone number
        if (nameaddress.Phone === '' || nameaddress.Phone === null){
            // default phone number to the return return address
            nameaddress.Phone = '(508) 650-2008';
        }

        if(nameaddress.Email !== null){
            var userEmail = nameaddress.Email;
            var senderName = 'Zyno Medical';
            
            // general visibility
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CarrierMonitoring= true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].PriorDeliveryNotificationConsignee = true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].NotificationFailureAddressEmail = userEmail;

            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Shipment Notification";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // delivery notification
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Delivery Notification"
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // delivery exeption notification
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Delivery Exeption Notification";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // return delivery notification
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Return Delivery Notification"
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationDescription = '';
           
            // remove the email field from the consignee
            nameaddress.Email = '';
        }
    }
